on note{thread-unsafe}
	ignore_event(EVENT_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{int}, 1){Builtin, None}
	group_count001{int} := 0
	v00{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(in_range(EVENT_NOTE{int}, keyswitch_octave{int} * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{int}) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{int} - 1)) 
			group_count001{int} := _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int}
			_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}]{int}
			if(group_count001{int} # _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int})
				v00{int} := TRUE{int}
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{int} := i{int}
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(v00{int} = TRUE{int})
			idx00002{int} := idx000000{int}
			call c_update_keyswitch_selection0{UserDefined, Call}
		end if
	end if
	if(pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} = - 1)
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		last_pressed[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		key_velocity[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := EVENT_VELOCITY{int}
		inc(num_pressed_keys{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
	last_on_note_callback{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	wait_time0{int} := note_selection_time{int} * 1000
	call c_wait_or_zero0{UserDefined, Call}
	if(last_on_note_callback{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
		ks20{int} := v00{int}
		result000{int} := group_count001{int}
		i400{int} := idx000000{int}
		articulation_event_id001{int} := articulation_event_id000{int}
		set_articulation_event_id001{int} := set_articulation_event_id000{int}
		next_free_idx0001{int} := next_free_idx0000{int}
		idx3001{int} := idx3000{int}
		i3001{int} := i3000{int}
		is_free0001{int} := is_free0000{int}
		_ret110001{int} := _ret110000{int}
		result10001{int} := result10000{int}
		call c_update_selected_notes0{UserDefined, Call}
	end if
end on

on release{thread-unsafe}
	if(get_event_mark(EVENT_ID{int}, MARK_1{int}){Builtin, None} = FALSE{int})
		set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{int}, 0){Builtin, None}
		last_release_callback{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
		ignore_event(EVENT_ID{int}){Builtin, None}
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{int}]{int} := - 1
		dec(num_pressed_keys{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(sustain_pedal{int} = OFF{int})
			message("added note off event to queue"){Builtin, None}
			instrument_slot1{int} := 0
			note2{int} := EVENT_NOTE{int}
			ks10{int} := idx000000{int}
			i50{int} := group_count001{int}
			_ret1000{int} := v00{int}

function c_is_in_note_selection0
	result01{int} := FALSE{int}
	select(note_selection0{int})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_OFF{int}
		result01{int} := TRUE{int}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST{int}

		end if
	end if
end function

			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[idx001{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[idx001{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(idx001{int}){Builtin, None}

	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "    Empty"){Builtin, None}
	end if
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_solo_subarticulation{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _subarticulations_solo_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}

	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}, int(round(real(int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} + (real(int((real(_articulation_volume_max[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None} - int((real(_articulation_volume_min[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} * pow(real(i{int}){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, (real(_articulation_volume_curve[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}

		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}

			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}

		end if

	end while

	while(i{int} <= (num_elements(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}){Builtin, None} - 1))

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} # - 1)
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(i{int} = selected_subarticulation{int})
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, 127 - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_dynamic_range_control
	xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_cursor{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - 5) + int((real(((modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} * (1 + (sh_right(127 - modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (1 * sh_right(modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})) - (127 * sh_right(127 - modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function c_angle_to_value0
	new_angle00{real} := angle2{real} + (NI_MATH_PI{real} / 2)
	if(new_angle00{real} > (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2))
		new_angle00{real} := new_angle00{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})
	end if
	new_angle00{real} := abs(new_angle00{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})){Builtin, None}
	ret130{int} := int((127 * (new_angle00{real} - angle_min0{real})) / (angle_max0{real} - angle_min0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function
